His breathing slowed, becoming steady and controlled. The tension in his muscles gradually eased as he immersed himself in the tranquility of meditation. Images of his goals and aspirations flickered behind closed eyelids, driving him to push harder, to prove himself beyond any doubt.

His cloak billowed behind him, adding to his imposing figure, and his icy gaze swept across the arena, taking in every detail with a keen awareness. The sinister smirk on his face played at the corners of his lips, a subtle promise of impending action and calculated moves.

With a deliberate motion, Sogeki cracked his knuckles one by one, the sound echoing faintly in the silence. It was a gesture of readiness, a physical manifestation of the energy coursing through him. His eyes narrowed slightly, focusing on the challengers gathered in the arena, each one a potential obstacle to overcome.

A low murmur of anticipation rippled through the crowd as they sensed the imminent clash of wills. Some regarded him with apprehension, others with curiosity, but all acknowledged his presence with a mixture of respect and wariness.

Without a word, Sogeki positioned himself at the center of the arena, his stance firm and balanced. He exuded an aura of dominance and readiness, a silent challenge to anyone bold enough to face him. With a swift sidestep and a flick of his wrist, Sogeki manages to deflect some of the senbon, but one grazes his shoulder, drawing a sharp intake of breath from him. He winces at the pain but doesn&#39;t falter. His mind races, recalibrating his approach as he continues his determined advance towards Higane.

His strategy remains unchanged: assert dominance, prove his strength, and seize control of the confrontation. The unfamiliar technique Higane mentioned is momentarily set aside in his mind as he readies himself for the next exchange, focused on the immediate challenge before him.
